Total outgoing passengers served: 1000

======================================================================
INCOMING FLIGHT SYNCHRONIZATIONS (with Demand)
======================================================================
  Flight 2 → Train 3 at Station 1: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=526, train_dep=563.0, transfer=37.0min, penalty=3.20
  Flight 24 → Train 4 at Station 3: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=697, train_dep=747.0, transfer=50.0min, penalty=6.00
  Flight 26 → Train 5 at Station 3: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=863, train_dep=908.0, transfer=45.0min, penalty=0.00
  Flight 17 → Train 6 at Station 2: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=1037, train_dep=1082.0, transfer=45.0min, penalty=0.00

Total incoming synchronizations: 4
Total incoming passengers served: 400

 Could not import visualization modules: No module named 'visualization_module'
Make sure these files are in your directory:
  • visualization_module.py
  • advanced_demand_visualization.py
